[30;1m128 | [0m[35mQuerySet Updates with History (Updated in Django 2.2)[0m
[30;1m129 | [0m[35m~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[0m
[30;1m130 | [0m[35mUnlike with ``bulk_create``, `queryset updates`_ perform an SQL update query on[0m
[30;1m131 | [0m[35mthe queryset, and never return the actual updated objects (which would be[0m
[30;1m132 | [0m[35mnecessary for the inserts into the historical table). Thus, we tell you that[0m
[30;1m133 | [0m[35mqueryset updates will not save history (since no ``post_save`` signal is sent).[0m

[30;1m4 | [0m[35mBulk Creating and Queryset Updating[0m
[30;1m5 | [0m[35m-----------------------------------[0m

[30;1m10 | [0m[35m``django-simple-history`` provides utility functions to work around this.[0m
